## Defenses & Compensatory Mechanisms

# UATU DOSSIER — SECTION 7

## Defenses & Compensatory Mechanisms

*Subject: Zemo, Heinrich, Baron XII. Defensive architecture, longitudinal, ranked by primitiveness per Vaillant/Kernberg hierarchies, cross-indexed to observed behavior across the published record (Sgt. Fury #8; Tales of Suspense #60–68; Avengers #4–15; Captain America #168, #275–278; Citizen V/V-Battalion retrospectives; Thunderbolts continuity for posthumous corroboration).*

---

### 7.0 Preface: How the Defenses Are Organized

The subject does not run a balanced defensive economy. His architecture is **bottom-heavy** — primitive defenses (splitting, projection, omnipotence, denial, somatization-by-bonding) dominate the load; neurotic defenses (intellectualization, reaction formation, displacement) handle middle traffic; mature defenses (sublimation, humor, anticipation, altruism) are nearly absent or, where present, are degraded forms wearing mature clothing. The single mature defense that genuinely operates is **sublimation**, and even it has been hijacked, after Adhesive X, by the obsessional revenge program and ceases to function as containment.

This bottom-heaviness is itself the diagnostic shape of malignant narcissism. The defenses are not failing — they are doing precisely what defenses do; they are simply primitive enough that their byproducts (cruelty, escalation, monothematic fixation, sensory armor) become the subject's recognizable behavioral fingerprint.

Rank order below proceeds from most primitive (Level 1) to most mature (Level 4), with each defense traced to specific canonical operations.

---

### 7.1 LEVEL 1 — PRIMITIVE / PSYCHOTIC-ADJACENT DEFENSES

These run continuously, ego-syntonically, and below conscious access.

#### 7.1.1 Splitting (Kleinian / Kernbergian sense)

The foundational defense and the one whose failure modes generate the entire late-career escalation. The world is sorted, without intermediates, into:

- **The worthy:** Zemos, the bloodline, the Reich (ideologically), the rare instrumentally useful peer (Enchantress as goddess-asset), demonstrated technical mastery.
- **The contemptible:** serfs, native labor in the Amazon base, captured subordinates after they fail, Americans-as-a-category, the disfigured face beneath the hood (split off and treated as not-self).

The instability of the split shows in his treatment of **Captain America**, who occupies both poles simultaneously: a contemptible American soldier-pawn (lower pole) AND a singular, world-defining adversary worth the entire remaining life (upper pole). Healthy splitting allows the enemy to be wholly devalued; pathological splitting against a single object oscillates, and the oscillation is the obsessional engine. Each time Zemo devalues Cap intellectually ("a mere soldier") he generates a contradiction with the operational reality (this mere soldier destroyed my lab, my face, my life), and the contradiction reignites the campaign.

Behavioral signature: every recorded monologue toggles within sentences between contempt for Cap and obsession with Cap. The toggle is the tell.

#### 7.1.2 Projection (specifically: projection of agency and projection of the wound)

Heinrich's lab was destroyed because Heinrich was a senior weapons designer for a regime at war; Cap was the responding combatant. The disfigurement is, in the chain of causation, an industrial accident of war initiated by the subject's own enterprise. The defense erases this by relocating agency entirely onto Cap: *Cap did this to me*, where the verb "did" carries malice, intention, and personal vendetta that the actual event does not support.

This is not delusion (Section 4 covered the distinction) — Zemo can recite the facts. It is projection: the **meaning** of agency is exported. The self cannot tolerate being the author of its own ruin, so authorship is donated to the only available recipient.

Secondary projection: the wounded contempt for his own face is projected onto every face he sees. He treats subordinates with the disgust he cannot direct at his mirrorless self.

#### 7.1.3 Omnipotent Control / Devaluation

The Masters of Evil convocations (Avengers #6, #7, etc.) read, on the surface, as recruitment. Structurally they are theaters of omnipotent control: the subject summons, deploys, and discards. The Black Knight (Garrett), Melter, Radioactive Man, Enchantress, Executioner — none of them are mourned when lost, none are sought out for rescue, none are addressed as peers. They are extensions of the subject's will, and when they fail they are devalued instantly into "incompetents" rather than mourned as comrades.

Devaluation is also the principal weapon Zemo turns against his own internal states. Pain from the hood interface — devalued as beneath notice. The longing for an unmasked face — devalued as weakness. Helmut's developmental needs for paternal warmth — devalued as childishness to be drilled out.

#### 7.1.4 Primitive Idealization (transient, of the bloodline)

The Zemo line is idealized as biologically and historically superior. This is not the same as splitting — splitting concerns objects in the present field; idealization is the static elevation of an abstraction. The bloodline functions as the **idealized self-object** that the subject's grandiosity attaches to. Helmut inherits this as a sacred trust; the V-Battalion antagonism is read by Heinrich as confirmation that the line is significant enough to have hereditary enemies of stature.

The idealization is necessary because the **actual** self — disfigured, fugitive, hunted, jungle-bound, hood-bonded — cannot be idealized without manifest contradiction. The bloodline absorbs the idealization the self can no longer hold.

#### 7.1.5 Denial (of the wound-as-wound)

Zemo never, in the published record, refers to the Adhesive X bonding as a *catastrophe* or an *injury*. He refers to its consequences (the need for vengeance) and its operational meaning (the mark of his war with Cap). The event itself is denied as an event of suffering. This is denial in the strict sense — not denial of fact, but denial of affective weight.

The hood is reframed: not "the thing I cannot remove" but "the instrument by which I terrify." The somatic horror — that he cannot eat, drink, sleep, wash, or be touched normally for the remainder of his life — is excluded from speech and presumably from internal narration. The denial is so total that we have no canonical instance of him acknowledging the cowl as an object on his body at all; he wears it as if it were always-already his face.

#### 7.1.6 Somatization-in-Reverse (the hood as enacted defense)

A specialized item. Most somatization converts psychic conflict into bodily symptom. Heinrich's case is structurally inverted: an actual bodily catastrophe is conscripted into a psychic defense. The hood, having become his body, is *used* as a defense — it physically prevents the encounter (with mirror, with intimate other, with the recognizable face of Heinrich Zemo the man) that would force integration of the wound. The injury has been recruited as armor against the meaning of the injury.

This is why no surgeon's intervention would have been welcomed even if available. Removing the hood would remove the defense. The bonding is not only a tragedy that happened to him; it has become a tragedy he requires.

---

### 7.2 LEVEL 2 — IMMATURE DEFENSES

#### 7.2.1 Passive Aggression — *largely absent.*

Notable by absence. Heinrich's aggression is active, declared, signed. He does not sulk, sabotage covertly, or weaponize delay. The absence is consistent with the aristocratic-grandiose substrate: passive-aggression is the weapon of subordinates, and the subject does not experience himself as subordinate to anyone living.

#### 7.2.2 Acting Out

Heavily present in the late career. The Adhesive X-over-Manhattan scheme (Avengers #15) is acting out at industrial scale: an intolerable internal state (the conjoined rage-shame of repeated defeats) is discharged through external action against a civilian population chosen because it baits the enemy. The choice of weapon — Adhesive X, the same substance that bonded the hood — is acting out at the level of symbol: he proposes to inflict on a city what was inflicted on his head. The act is more communication than strategy.

The terminal hillside pursuit is also acting out — affect (humiliation at the latest failure) discharged into motor activity (the chase) without strategic mediation.

#### 7.2.3 Fantasy (schizoid retreat)

The jungle base in the Amazon is, beyond its operational function, a fantasy-retreat. There Heinrich is the lord of all he surveys — native labor as serfs, laboratory as castle, the world reduced to a court of one. The geography of the base reconstructs in miniature the aristocratic universe the war destroyed. He could have operated from any number of more strategically sensible locations; he chose a jungle in which he could be feudal again.

#### 7.2.4 Projective Identification (toward Helmut)

Distinct from projection. Heinrich does not merely externalize unwanted contents onto Helmut; he **shapes Helmut into a recipient who behaves them out**. The son becomes the unconscious-aggressive avenger of the father's wound, taking up the campaign Heinrich could not complete. Helmut's adult identity (Captain America #275ff; Thunderbolts) is the projective-identification yield: the father's ungrieved injury, walking around in a son's body, wearing a copy of the father's hood by choice rather than necessity. This is among the most efficient projective identifications in the published record of supervillainy: the recipient does not merely carry the projection; he *organizes his entire identity* around it.

#### 7.2.5 Devaluation as Affect Regulation

Distinct from the omnipotent devaluation of subordinates (7.1.3). This is the moment-to-moment use of contempt as a thermoregulator on internal states. Every threatened experience of shame, fear, longing, or grief is met with an immediate contemptuous reframe directed outward: *they are unworthy, the era is debased, the enemy is beneath me*. The contempt is the temperature control.

---

### 7.3 LEVEL 3 — NEUROTIC DEFENSES

#### 7.3.1 Intellectualization

The technical-scientific career is partly genuine talent (the Adhesive X work is real) and partly the largest intellectualization in his life. Affect that would otherwise be experienced as shame, terror, or grief is rerouted through laboratory work, into formulae, mechanisms, deployment plans. The lab is where feeling becomes a problem of synthesis.

This explains why the post-disfigurement schemes are technically baroque (disintegrator pistols, chemical attack vectors, exotic recruits) far beyond what a strategically minded operator would deploy. The complexity is doing affective work: each new device is another container for the otherwise unbearable.

#### 7.3.2 Reaction Formation (mild, around the wound)

The hood is presented as *chosen menace* — the opposite of the truth (it is unchosen disfigurement). The presentation reverses the polarity of the experience. He stands taller in it than he likely stood unmasked. The cowl is worn the way a deformed limb is sometimes amputated to its prosthesis: the prosthesis is brandished as if it were the original organ improved.

#### 7.3.3 Displacement

Rage at the Reich's collapse, at the lost laboratory at home, at the lost aristocratic order, at his own face — all displaced onto Cap. Cap absorbs every loss the subject sustained between 1944 and his death. He is metabolizing the destruction of an entire world by treating it as the personal grievance of one man against one man.

The displacement is functional in the sense that it gives the subject a tractable target; it is corrosive in that the target cannot possibly satisfy the load placed on him. Even Cap's death would not return the laboratory at home, the bloodline's pre-war station, or the face beneath the cowl. The displacement is therefore structurally insatiable, which is why the program runs until death.

#### 7.3.4 Isolation of Affect

Heinrich can discuss the bonding, the war, the casualties, his subordinates' losses, with no audible affect. The facts are spoken; the feelings are sequestered. This is classical isolation, and it is what makes him appear, in monologue, as the controlled aristocratic menace rather than the operationally desperate man he actually is. The composure is a defense, not a temperament.

#### 7.3.5 Undoing (failed, attempted)

Every Masters of Evil convocation is, beneath the operational frame, an attempt at undoing — to cancel the prior defeat by overlaying a victory on top of it. Undoing in the classical Freudian sense requires symbolic reversal; what Heinrich attempts is literal reversal: *defeat Cap and the prior defeat is annulled*. This is undoing operating without the symbolic mediation that would allow it to succeed; each failed attempt therefore generates additional material requiring further undoing. The defense compounds its own debt.

#### 7.3.6 Identification (with the Aggressor, developmentally; with the Dynasty, structurally)

The cruelty the subject received as a child of the Zemo line is identified-with and re-transmitted — to subordinates, to native labor, to Helmut. The dynastic ideal is identified-with so completely that the subject ceases to have a personal identity distinct from "Baron Zemo, twelfth of the line." When asked, implicitly, who he is, the answer is a position in a sequence, not a person.

This is identification operating as identity-substitution. The personal self is so thinly developed (or so thoroughly evacuated into the hood and the bloodline) that the inherited role fills the space the self would otherwise occupy.

---

### 7.4 LEVEL 4 — MATURE DEFENSES

#### 7.4.1 Sublimation (genuine, then captured)

Pre-disfigurement, the scientific career is real sublimation: aggressive and grandiose energies channeled into legitimate (within the criminal frame of the regime) intellectual production. The Adhesive X work is the artifact of a man capable of mature defensive operation when his world is intact.

Post-disfigurement, sublimation is captured by the revenge program. The lab serves the obsession; the obsession does not serve the lab. The defense persists in form (he is still building things) but loses its containment function (the things built are all weapons against one man). This is the degradation of a mature defense into an instrument of a primitive one.

#### 7.4.2 Anticipation — *minimal.*

He plans tactically (recruitment, ambush, weapon deployment) but does not anticipate emotionally. He does not prepare himself for the possibility of failure or for the affective costs of victory. Each defeat arrives as fresh narcissistic injury rather than as a contingency previously rehearsed. The poverty of anticipation is why the escalations are unbounded — he never models the world in which the obsession concludes.

#### 7.4.3 Humor — *absent.*

No recorded instance of humor, wit, irony at his own expense, or play. The absence is itself diagnostic: humor requires the capacity to hold the self lightly, and the subject's self cannot be held lightly without falling apart. The cowl, were it only a costume, might admit a wry remark; because it is the body, no remark is possible.

#### 7.4.4 Altruism — *absent, with one apparent exception that is not one.*

Helmut might be argued as a target of paternal investment, hence altruism. The argument fails: the investment is ideological reproduction, not care. The child receives indoctrination, expectation, and the burden of the dynasty; he does not receive warmth, attunement, or any act undertaken for his benefit independent of the line's continuation. This is dynastic investment, not altruism.

#### 7.4.5 Suppression — *partial.*

He suppresses certain affects (visible fear, visible grief, sexual interest beyond instrumental courtship of Enchantress) to maintain the controlled aristocratic presentation. Suppression here is a thin layer over the more primitive isolation and denial; it is the surface finish, not the structural mechanism.

---

### 7.5 COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS — POSITIVE / FUNCTIONAL

These are the capacities and outputs that the defensive architecture, despite its primitiveness, allows him to maintain.

- **Scientific productivity.** Even disfigured, fugitive, and jungle-bound, he continues to design and to build. The Adhesive X work survives the war; the disintegrator pistol he carries at his death is presumably his own design. Productivity is preserved.
- **Operational command capacity.** He can recruit, brief, deploy, and coordinate enhanced and divine assets. The Masters of Evil function as a unit, however briefly, which is non-trivial managerially.
- **Physical self-maintenance into late age.** He engages Cap physically in his late 50s/60s. Muscular and cardiovascular fitness are maintained — likely an aristocratic-ascetic regimen, possibly the only domain where the body is treated as something he still owns.
- **Composure under stress.** The isolation and suppression deliver a recognizable phenotype — the cold, articulate, unhurried aristocrat — that functions as social armor in negotiation and as terror-induction in combat.
- **Dynastic continuity.** The grooming of Helmut, however cold, succeeds in producing a son willing and able to carry the project forward. As reproductive strategy this is functional, even if as fatherhood it is monstrous.
- **Concealment and operational security.** The Amazon base is never penetrated except in pursuit. He understands logistics, supply, perimeter, and the value of geographic remoteness.

---

### 7.6 COMPENSATORY MECHANISMS — NEGATIVE / CORROSIVE

These are the price the defensive architecture exacts, and they accumulate.

- **The obsessional revenge program itself.** The single largest negative compensation. It absorbs all resources — scientific, financial, temporal, relational, somatic — into a project that cannot succeed in its true (unconscious) aim of restoring the self.
- **Trophy-keeping.** Bucky Barnes' mask. The single most psychologically dense object in his possession. It functions as: (a) proof-of-power against the implicit accusation of impotence, (b) talisman against the humiliation of repeated defeats by Bucky's partner, (c) **manufactured symmetry** with Cap — Zemo needs Cap to want him dead as urgently as he wants Cap dead, and the mask is the physical guarantor that he has given Cap a reason. The trophy is the negotiated currency of a relationship Cap has not actually entered. It also functions as self-administered humiliation, since the same artifact records the success that produced the enemy that produced the wound.
- **Recruitment-and-discard pattern.** Each Masters of Evil convocation burns reputational capital among the supervillain ecology. He is increasingly known as a principal who does not protect his subordinates. Recruitment quality necessarily degrades over time; the move toward divine assets (Enchantress, Executioner) reflects not ambition but the exhaustion of mortal options.
- **Geographic and political exile.** The jungle base is a fortress and a tomb. He has no embassy, no court, no return path to European aristocratic society. The bloodline ideal is increasingly disconnected from any soil on which it could be reconstituted.
- **Affective constriction.** No friendships, no love, no recorded pleasure. The defensive architecture has so thoroughly insulated the self that there is no longer a self capable of receiving warmth even were it offered. This is the loss the subject does not register as loss.
- **The inability to disengage.** The escalation ladder runs upward because the defenses do not include the option of *stopping*. There is no defensive mechanism in his architecture that produces the affect of *enough*. Satiety would require mourning, which is precisely what denial and isolation prohibit.
- **The terminal recklessness.** The hillside pursuit on foot, firing a disintegrator wildly enough to trigger his own rockslide, is the defensive architecture in its final form: acting out, omnipotent control, denial of vulnerability, and refusal to anticipate, all operating simultaneously. He dies because his defenses have eliminated the capacity to recognize a moment in which retreat would be appropriate.
- **The bequest to the son.** Helmut inherits not only the title and the science but the whole defensive architecture, slightly modernized. The negative compensation extends past the subject's death into a second generation, and arguably beyond.

---

### 7.7 RANK-ORDERED SUMMARY

Most load-bearing defenses, in descending operational importance to the subject's daily functioning:

1. **Splitting** — the architectural foundation; every other defense is built on its bifurcated world.
2. **Denial (of the wound-as-wound)** — without it, the self cannot remain organized for an hour.
3. **Projection of agency onto Cap** — converts an unbearable authorship into a workable enmity.
4. **Somatization-in-reverse (the hood as enacted armor)** — the body itself enlisted as defense.
5. **Devaluation / omnipotent control** — manages the social field and the internal thermostat.
6. **Intellectualization (the laboratory)** — the largest legitimate container for displaced affect.
7. **Displacement (of all losses onto Cap)** — makes a tractable target out of a world-sized grief.
8. **Identification with the dynasty** — substitutes a role for a missing personal self.
9. **Projective identification (into Helmut)** — extends the project beyond the subject's lifespan.
10. **Sublimation (degraded)** — preserves productive capacity even as it serves the obsession.
11. **Isolation of affect / suppression** — delivers the public phenotype.
12. **Reaction formation (the hood reframed as menace chosen)** — small but visible.
13. **Undoing (perpetually failing)** — generates the schemes one after another.
14. **Fantasy (the feudal jungle court)** — reconstructs the lost world in miniature.
15. **Acting out (terminal-stage)** — discharges what the rest can no longer hold.

---

### 7.8 Coda: The Architecture Considered as a Whole

What this assemblage describes is a man whose defenses are exactly powerful enough to keep him functioning at a high operational level and exactly primitive enough to ensure that the functioning is monomaniacal, unsustainable, and terminal. The bottom-heaviness is not a flaw in the design; it *is* the design. A more mature defensive economy would have permitted mourning — and mourning would have dissolved the obsession, and the obsession is the only structure holding the post-Adhesive X self together. The defenses are not protecting a self that exists beneath them; **they are the self**, in the only form it has been able to take since the vat ruptured.

This is why no defeat reaches him as information and no victory would satisfy him: the architecture is not in the service of any underlying person whose welfare could be advanced or harmed. The person was the lab, the face, and the pre-war bloodline. What walks the Amazon in a bonded purple cowl is the defensive structure that survived him, wearing his name, his title, and his son's future like a uniform.


## Longitudinal Psychological Profile

# LONGITUDINAL PSYCHOLOGICAL PROFILE — BARON HEINRICH ZEMO

*Decade-by-decade reconstruction of affect regulation, cognitive style, and self-concept. Derived from canonical behavior, dynastic context, and the somatic record. Frameworks: Kernberg (object-relations / narcissistic structure), Bowlby/Main (attachment), Linehan (affect regulation as skill-set), Beck (cognitive schemas), Horowitz (stress-response states), Mullen/Meloy (grievance/fixated-persecutor literature), Erikson (psychosocial stages) where the developmental scaffolding warrants it.*

---

## I. CHILDHOOD AND LATE LATENCY (approx. ages 0–12; first decade of life on the Zemo estate, central Europe, pre-WWI)

### Affect regulation

The earliest extrapolable affective environment is the Zemo schloss: an aristocratic household in a line documented (V-Battalion material) as habitually cruel to dependents across twelve generations. Affect in such houses is regulated by *suppression and display rule* — a child is permitted the affects appropriate to rank (cold disdain, controlled anger at inferiors, ceremonial pride) and punished for those incompatible with it (fear, tenderness toward servants, grief, exuberant play). The absence anywhere in the adult record of laughter, tears, or warmth is not adult acquisition; it is the residue of a childhood in which those affects were extinguished early.

By the Linehan schema, the household functions as a *pervasively invalidating environment* of the aristocratic variant: the child's primary affects are not denied so much as *re-labeled* as moral failures of breeding. Crying is weakness; affection for a groom is degradation; fear is plebeian. The child develops not the borderline pattern (where the invalidating environment is chaotic) but its mirror image — overcontrolled, brittle, with all affect routed through a single permitted channel of cold contempt.

### Cognitive style

The technical brilliance shown in adulthood is not adventitious; it requires a childhood of intense, supported intellectual training — tutors, laboratories, the classical European pedagogy that produces both Heisenbergs and von Brauns. The cognitive style being trained is *analytic-systematic, hierarchical, deductive from first principles*. There is no record (and the household type does not generate) the kind of associative, playful, lateral cognition that comes from peer rough-and-tumble. He is being built into an instrument of high focal intelligence with poor peripheral vision — a cognitive architecture that will, decades later, prove unable to *notice* that all his plans are the same plan.

### Self-concept

Erikson's stages collapse strangely in dynastic children. *Trust vs. mistrust* is resolved not through caregiver responsiveness but through the reliable presence of the *name* — the bloodline is the secure base, more reliable than any mother. *Autonomy vs. shame* is short-circuited because shame is preloaded onto everything not-noble; the child cannot fail at being a Zemo, only at being insufficiently one. *Initiative* is rewarded only in domains that flatter the line.

The emergent self-concept at the end of latency is: *I am the twelfth instance of a thing that has existed for centuries, and my worth is measured by my fidelity to that thing.* This is the foundation of every subsequent pathology. The self is not first-person; it is genealogical. There is no "Heinrich" beneath the Baron-in-waiting, and there never will be.

---

## II. ADOLESCENCE AND EARLY ADULTHOOD (approx. ages 13–25; gymnasium and university years, pre- and inter-war)

### Affect regulation

The overcontrolled pattern consolidates. Adolescence in such households is not a period of identity exploration but of *grooming into station* — fencing salles, dueling societies (the *Mensur* tradition is plausible context), officer-cadet protocols, the etiquette of receiving and giving insult. These institutions teach affect regulation as *ritualized display*: rage is permitted only through formal channels (the duel, the cold rebuke), and the cost of leakage is social annihilation.

He emerges in his early twenties with an affect register that is essentially binary: ceremonial composure and ritualized aggression. The middle band — playfulness, ordinary warmth, ordinary sadness, ordinary fear — has atrophied from disuse, in the way a muscle atrophies. By the time he reaches the laboratory in his late twenties, those affects are not available to him as conscious options.

### Cognitive style

The university years are where the genuine first-rank scientific talent is consolidated. The Adhesive X work of the 1940s implies a foundational education in physical chemistry, polymer science, and adhesion physics that places him in the rare top tier of pre-war German-language chemistry. The cognitive style sharpens: he becomes a *closure-driven* problem solver (Kruglanski's need-for-closure framework applies) — high tolerance for short-term frustration in service of a defined endpoint, low tolerance for open-ended ambiguity. This is the cognitive substrate that later cannot leave Captain America unresolved.

A second feature begins to show: *the conflation of intellectual achievement with personal worth*. The bloodline self-concept absorbs the new datum — *I am brilliant* — and reorganizes around two pillars rather than one. This binarization is structurally fragile; if either pillar is struck, the other must bear the full load.

### Self-concept

The grandiosity becomes operationally grounded. In childhood the worth was inherited; in early adulthood it is *demonstrated*. He becomes, in Kernberg's terms, a *successful pathological narcissist* — the grandiose self is no longer purely defensive, because the world is in fact handing him evidence of superiority (academic prizes, family rank, intellectual deference). This is the most dangerous developmental moment for a narcissistic structure: when reality colludes, the structure becomes ego-syntonic and the person stops noticing it is a structure.

---

## III. THE THIRTIES (the Reich years, weapons-program career, marriage and fatherhood)

### Affect regulation

Three pressures converge: (1) the regime's ideological apparatus, which validates and amplifies the dynastic-supremacist substrate; (2) the operational demands of senior scientific-military command, requiring sustained controlled aggression; and (3) the formation of the only intimate relationships of his life — the unnamed mother of Helmut, and Helmut himself.

The marriage is canonically a cipher. The complete absence of the wife from any flashback, reminiscence, or named-relationship reference across the entire Zemo corpus (extending through Helmut's appearances in *Captain America* #275ff and the *Thunderbolts* runs, where one would expect a mother to surface in characterization) tells us something specific: she was either (a) dynastically selected, affectively peripheral, and died early, or (b) present in life but absent in his interior. Either way, the affect-regulation function that a spouse can provide — co-regulation, witness, the loosening of overcontrol in private — never came online. He enters fatherhood with the same brittle binary register.

Helmut, born in this decade, becomes the only sustained intimate object of Heinrich's life. The grooming pattern that produces the adult Helmut — fanatical filial devotion despite the absence of recorded warmth — is consistent with the *cold-grooming* pattern documented in dynastic and ideological families: affection is replaced by initiation, approval is rationed and conditional on adherence to the program, and the child's hunger for the withheld warmth is converted into loyalty. Heinrich, in this decade, is not affectively *cruel* to his son in the way he is to subordinates; he is something colder — *uninterested in him except as continuation*. The boy is a project, not a person.

### Cognitive style

This is the productive peak. The closure-driven, systematic intelligence is now operating with state resources, military application, and ideological permission to ignore ethical constraints. Adhesive X is the artifact. Cognitively, the work shows the signature of a problem-solver willing to brute-force a single hard problem (a polymer with no solvent) over years, which is again the closure-style.

The first cognitive *blind spots* of the adult pathology also harden here. He is operating inside a regime whose strategic stupidity will destroy it within fifteen years, and there is no record of him noticing or hedging. This is consistent with the broader pattern: high focal intelligence, poor peripheral vision, susceptibility to ideological frames that flatter the self-concept.

### Self-concept

The two pillars — bloodline and intellect — are now joined by a third: *historical mission*. He is not merely a brilliant Zemo; he is a brilliant Zemo *at the hinge of history*, building weapons for the New Order. The grandiose self has annexed the regime as a stage. This is the high-water mark of the integrated grandiose self; everything after is decompensation.

Helmut is, from this perspective, the *fourth* pillar: the continuance of the bloodline as an explicit project. The boy is loved precisely to the extent that he is recognized as instrumental to dynastic persistence, which is to say not at all in the way the boy needs.

---

## IV. THE FORTIES — THE FRACTURE DECADE (war years; partisan disfigurement; adoption of the hood; Bucky/Cap operation; Adhesive X bonding; flight to South America)

This is the decade in which the structure breaks and is rebuilt as the pathology proper.

### Affect regulation — early decade

Through the early war years he is operating at the productive peak of the previous decade. The Cap/Bucky operation in 1945 — the unmanned drone plane — is *strategically effective* as a single act; he killed Bucky and removed Cap from the war. As a piece of operational design it is competent and unsentimental. Note that even at this peak, the satisfaction is not recorded as celebrated — there is no canon of Heinrich enjoying the kill. The keeping of Bucky's mask as a trophy *originates here* and will be reinterpreted across the rest of his life: at the moment of acquisition it is a war souvenir, no different from a captured flag; only later does it become the fetish.

### The first injury — partisan disfigurement

The face injuries from partisan/Resistance attack are the first crack. The affective response — immediate, permanent masking — is disproportionate to the *probable* objective disfigurement (most facial scarring does not require permanent concealment), and tells us the wound was experienced narcissistically rather than medically. *To be seen damaged is worse than to be damaged.* The hood at this stage is voluntary, removable, theatrical — chosen partly as a fear instrument, partly as concealment, partly (and this is the underdeveloped reading) as a *pre-emptive* solution to a self-concept that has begun to feel exposed by the war turning against the Reich.

This is the moment at which his affect regulation begins to depend on a *prosthesis*. He can no longer hold his composure without the hood. The overcontrolled binary register has begun to leak, and the cloth holds it in.

### The second injury — Adhesive X bonding

The lab destruction and the vat rupture are the catastrophic event. The behavioral evidence is unambiguous about what happens to the psychological structure in that afternoon:

- *The narcissistic injury is total.* All four pillars (bloodline, intellect, mission, dynastic continuance) are struck simultaneously. The bloodline is humiliated; the intellect's masterpiece has been the agent of his ruin; the mission has collapsed with the Reich; and the dynastic continuance is now contingent on a son being raised by a hooded fugitive in a jungle.
- *The structure does not collapse — it concentrates.* This is the diagnostic moment. A less rigid character would have decompensated into psychosis, depression, or suicide. A more flexible one would have begun the painful work of restructuring. Heinrich does neither. He executes the maneuver that defines the rest of his life: *the wound is denied as wound and recoded as agent*. Cap did this. Therefore Cap is the obstacle to wholeness. Therefore Cap's destruction restores wholeness.
- *Affect regulation is now hostage to a single object.* Where before the binary register (composure / ritualized aggression) was generally serviceable, now the aggression channel has a single permanent target and runs continuously. The composure channel is increasingly performative — held up for subordinates — and decreasingly available to him in private.

### Cognitive style — the lock-in

The closure-driven cognitive style now has its lifetime problem. The intelligence does not degrade; it *narrows*. Every problem becomes a sub-problem of the Cap problem. This is the moment at which "large enough to construct elaborate plans, not large enough to notice the plans are all the same plan" becomes the operative description.

### Self-concept — the prosthesis

The hood, bonded, becomes the *literal* prosthesis of a self that can no longer hold itself together unaided. The four pillars are still nominally standing, but the structure between them is supplied by the cowl. Take the hood off (hypothetically — it cannot be removed) and the self that emerges is a defeated, disfigured, unhoused old man whose regime is gone, whose face is ruined, and whose life's work poisoned him. He cannot tolerate that self for an instant. The cowl is what makes him continuously possible to himself.

### Late decade — South America

The flight to the jungle is not retreat; it is the construction of the operational base for the lifetime project. The decade ends with him established in the Amazon hideout, native labor in place, beginning the long preparation for an enemy who is (so far as he knows) dead. The fact that the preparation continues despite Cap's apparent death is the strongest possible evidence that the obsession is *intrapsychic* rather than reactive — he is preparing to kill Cap because he needs the project, not because he expects the target.

---

## V. THE FIFTIES (the South American interregnum; Helmut's adolescence at distance; the long preparation)

### Affect regulation

This is the decade of *encysted* affect. With no enemy present, no regime to serve, no court to perform for, the brittle binary register has nothing external to organize it. The behavioral record from this period is thin in canon, but the operational evidence — the maintenance of the base, the slow accumulation of resources, the continued scientific work — implies a man functioning on a kind of grim operational autopilot.

The affect that would normally surface in such conditions — boredom, loneliness, grief, doubt — is locked behind the hood. There is no one to perform composure for except the native laborers, whom he does not regard as audience. The likely interior state is what Horowitz would call a *frozen stress-response state*: chronic, low-grade dysphoria managed by ritualized work, somatic suppression, and the steady tending of the grievance like a hearth fire.

### Cognitive style

The narrowing continues. Without operational pressure to test his thinking against reality, the cognitive style becomes increasingly *ruminative-rehearsal*: he is planning the Cap operation over and over, refining schemes for an enemy who, so far as anyone knows, is at the bottom of the Atlantic. This is the cognitive pattern that the fixated-persecutor literature (Mullen et al.) identifies in long-incubation grievance cases — the target is mentally rehearsed into a more elaborate and more loathsome construct than the actual person ever was. By the time Cap is recovered in 1964, the Captain America that Heinrich has been fighting in his head for nearly twenty years is a vastly more important figure than the one Rogers actually is.

### Self-concept

The four pillars have effectively collapsed into one *operational identity*: I am the man who will kill Captain America. The bloodline survives as background piety; the intellect is conscripted; the mission has been replaced; the dynastic continuance is outsourced to Helmut at distance. This is the decade in which the diagnosis solidifies from *injured pathological narcissism* into *monothematic grievance-organized personality* — a self that has only one project, and is therefore no longer a self in the ordinary sense but a function.

### The fatherhood at distance

Helmut spends his adolescence in this decade with a hooded fugitive father in a jungle base, or visiting him from European schooling, or being indoctrinated by proxy through trusted couriers. The exact arrangement is not canonical, but the outcome — Helmut's adult fanaticism with no recorded warmth — implies an ideological inheritance delivered without intimacy. Heinrich, in this decade, is *teaching* the boy without *raising* him. The boy is being given the program. He is not being held.

---

## VI. THE SIXTIES — THE OPERATIONAL DECADE AND TERMINAL DECOMPENSATION (the Cap-recovered years; Masters of Evil convocations; death on the hillside)

### Affect regulation — controlled re-ignition

The recovery of Cap in *Avengers* #4 is, paradoxically, the best thing that happens to Heinrich in twenty years. The encysted affect now has a real-world target again. The binary register reactivates: ceremonial composure for the Masters of Evil (the hauteur that Garrett, the Melter, and Chen Lu would have encountered), ritualized aggression directed at Cap.

But the register is no longer holding cleanly. The affective leak that began with the partisan injury and accelerated with the bonding is now showing in the *operational* record:

- *Escalation without strategic warrant.* When the first Masters fail, a rational adversary regroups. He instead recruits Asgardians. When they fail, he attacks Manhattan with chemical weapons. The escalation is *affect-driven* — each defeat is experienced as a fresh narcissistic wound and demands a larger response.
- *Reduced tolerance for delegation.* The early Masters convocations have him directing from a distance; by #15 he is personally on the hillside with a sidearm. The composure channel is failing; he needs to do it himself.
- *Loss of dignity-management.* The aristocrat who would have preferred any other death dies running, firing wildly. The composure that held for sixty years finally breaks in the final minutes, and what was underneath it — a frantic, hooded old man who cannot stop — is briefly visible.

### Cognitive style — terminal narrowing

The cognitive narrowing reaches its endpoint. He can still plan tactically; he can no longer think strategically about anything except Cap. The Adhesive-X-over-Manhattan scheme is a useful diagnostic: as a *tactic for drawing Cap into a trap*, it is functional; as a *strategic act for any other purpose Heinrich Zemo might plausibly have* (Reich restoration, wealth, escape, retirement, anything), it is incoherent. He has no other purposes. The intelligence is intact but uni-directional.

### Self-concept — the prosthesis fails

The hood is still on; the self it has been holding together is increasingly held together *only* by the hood. The four pillars are now functionally one: the operational identity. When Cap, on the hillside, is about to escape him again, the self has nowhere to retreat to. There is no Heinrich beneath the project. The fall, the rockslide, the absurd unwitnessed death — this is the structure ending. It is fitting and consistent that he dies in pursuit; there is no other state in which the self could be found by that moment.

### Posthumous coda — the structure that did not die

The most important psychological fact about Heinrich Zemo's death is that it is *not* the end of his structure. Helmut, raised in the cold-grooming pattern of the thirties and fifties, carries the entire architecture forward — the dynastic grandiosity, the obsessional anti-Cap project, the racial-supremacist substrate, even the hood as identity-prosthesis. The pathology that Heinrich could not metabolize in his own life he successfully *transmitted*, which is the worst possible posthumous verdict: the structure was so total that it reproduced itself in another human being.

---

## VII. ACROSS-DECADE SYNTHESIS — THE THREE LONG ARCS

Three trajectories run the length of the life and clarify each other when overlaid.

**Arc 1: Affect regulation.** *Overcontrolled binary register (childhood–thirties) → prosthesis-dependent register (forties onward) → terminal leak (sixties).* The decline is not in capacity for control but in the resources required to maintain it. By the end he needs the hood, the jungle base, the rituals of command, and the active presence of the enemy to hold composure — and even then it fails on the hillside.

**Arc 2: Cognitive style.** *Closure-driven systematic brilliance (university–thirties) → narrowed to a single problem (forties) → ruminative-rehearsal lock-in (fifties) → tactically intact but strategically incoherent (sixties).* The intelligence does not deteriorate. Its aperture does. He dies as smart as he ever was, applied to a problem that cannot be solved by being smart.

**Arc 3: Self-concept.** *Genealogical self (childhood) → bloodline-plus-intellect (early adulthood) → four-pillar grandiose self (thirties) → prosthesis-dependent self organized around grievance (forties onward) → operational identity with no remainder (fifties–sixties) → unhoused self briefly visible at death.*

The three arcs are not independent. Each catastrophe in one accelerates the others. The partisan injury narrowed the cognition because it destabilized the self-concept and overloaded the affect register. The Adhesive X bonding locked all three together with a single piece of cloth. The recovery of Cap reactivated all three on a single object. The hillside is where all three end together, because by then they were no longer separable.

He spent sixty years becoming, with great effort and considerable intelligence, a man who could die only one way. He achieved it.


## Psychiatric Assessment & Differential

# PSYCHIATRIC ASSESSMENT & DIFFERENTIAL

## Subject: ZEMO, Heinrich — Baron, XII of the line

*Assessment compiled from longitudinal behavioral record, 1939–death; cross-referenced with collateral testimony from son (Helmut Zemo) and subordinate accounts (surviving Masters of Evil personnel, V-Battalion intelligence dossiers). No subject interview ever conducted; no formal psychometric instruments administered; all diagnostic formulation reverse-engineered from behavior, communications, and physical-trace evidence. Confidence intervals are accordingly qualified throughout.*

---

## I. SUMMARY DIAGNOSTIC IMPRESSION

A multiaxial, structural formulation rather than a single label. The subject presents, across a twenty-five-year observable window, with:

1. **Primary (Axis II analog): Narcissistic Personality Disorder, malignant subtype** (DSM-5-TR 301.81 / ICD-11 6D10.1 with prominent dissocial features). Kernberg-criteria malignant narcissism specifically — i.e., NPD + ego-syntonic aggression + paranoid features + sadism.
2. **Comorbid (Axis II analog): Antisocial Personality Disorder features**, sub-threshold for primary classification only because the disorganized-impulsive aspect of ASPD is absent; the cruelty is organized, dynastic, and ideologically scaffolded.
3. **Axis I analog: Persistent Complex Grievance-Revenge Syndrome**, monothematic, fixated, escalating — closer in structure to the forensic literature on grievance-driven fixated stalkers (Mullen, Pathé, Purcell) than to any ICD/DSM category proper. This is the *active* clinical picture; the personality disorder is the substrate, the grievance syndrome is the engine.
4. **Axis I analog: Unresolved Acute Stress reaction with somatic anchoring**, atypically organized into mission rather than the conventional intrusion/avoidance/hyperarousal triad. Not PTSD as written, but functionally analogous: a single, irreversible somatic event organizes the remainder of life.
5. **Axis III (medical, with psychiatric sequelae): Permanent dermal/subdermal fusion of cloth-cowl, chronic interface pain, chronic sensory occlusion**, with predictable contributions to irritability, sleep disturbance, sensory deprivation phenomena, and the continuous tactile reinforcement of the precipitating event.

The subject is **not** psychotic, **not** intellectually disabled, **not** organically demented, **not** primarily depressed, **not** primarily anxious, and — importantly, against superficial impression — **not** a classical primary psychopath. Differential below.

---

## II. PRIMARY DIAGNOSIS: NARCISSISTIC PERSONALITY DISORDER, MALIGNANT SUBTYPE

### A. DSM-5-TR Criterion Walk-Through

DSM requires five of nine. The subject satisfies all nine, which is itself diagnostically meaningful: the disorder is not partial or compensated but florid and structurally dominant.

**(1) Grandiose sense of self-importance.** Self-presentation as the bearer of a twelve-generation noble line; constant invocation of the Zemo name as a self-sufficient justification for action; the assumption, never argued, that his enmity confers significance on its object. Operational signature: introduces himself by title, never by function. Will not answer to "Heinrich" from a subordinate; will not tolerate the omission of "Baron" even in radio communications where brevity matters.

**(2) Preoccupation with fantasies of unlimited success, power, brilliance.** The serial reconvening of the Masters of Evil after each defeat. The escalation pattern — solo plot → small team → enhanced team → Asgardian divine assets → mass-casualty chemical attack on Manhattan — describes not a planner but a fantasist whose plans expand as the fantasy is frustrated. The Adhesive-X-over-Manhattan scheme is, technically, a *bait* — but the choice of bait reveals the underlying fantasy: a city paralyzed and silenced by his signature compound, with him at the center.

**(3) Belief in being "special" and unique.** The dynastic frame again; the refusal, even in extremis, to operate under cover identities or pseudonyms once disfigured (he does not become Smith of Brazil — he becomes Baron Zemo, in the jungle). The hood is adopted not for tactical concealment first but for the theatrical announcement of self.

**(4) Requires excessive admiration.** Recruitment patterns. The Masters of Evil are not selected by competence alone — the Enchantress recruitment in *Avengers* #7 brings him no tactical advantage commensurate with the risk of allying with an Asgardian; the value to him is being *seen with* Asgardian assets. Subordinates report (collateral) that meetings begin with extended exposition of his own scientific accomplishments before objectives are stated.

**(5) Sense of entitlement.** Treatment of indigenous labor at the Amazonian base as property. Disposal of subordinates with no transition ritual, no severance, no acknowledgment. The expectation that allies will subordinate their goals to his — which is why his coalitions fragment. Entitlement is the load-bearing wall; when it cracks, the whole structure shifts to rage.

**(6) Interpersonally exploitative.** Universal. Every named relationship in the record — Garrett, the Melter, Chen Lu, Amora, Skurge, the native staff, his son — functions as instrument. No counterexample exists in canon.

**(7) Lacks empathy.** Adhesive X on Manhattan is the cleanest demonstration. The chemical would have caused mass civilian asphyxiation and immobilization; the indifference is total. The treatment of Bucky Barnes — a teenage soldier whose mask is kept as a trophy decades later — also qualifies; the empathic register is unavailable even retrospectively.

**(8) Envious of others or believes others are envious of him.** Specifically directed at Captain America. The fixation has an envious topology — Cap possesses what Heinrich does not: a face, a moral position from which others extend warmth, the loyalty of comrades freely given. The recoding of these absences in himself as Cap's *crimes against him* is structurally envious.

**(9) Arrogant, haughty behaviors or attitudes.** Constant. The diction in recovered communications is uniformly imperious; the body comportment — even in surveillance photographs taken from concealment — shows a chin elevation and shoulder set characteristic of habitual rank display.

### B. The Malignant Specifier (Kernberg)

Kernberg's malignant narcissism requires NPD plus three additional features. All present.

- **Ego-syntonic aggression.** The cruelty is not experienced as conflictual. There is no recorded moment of guilt, hesitation, or after-the-fact rationalization. Aggression is felt as legitimate exercise of position.
- **Paranoid orientation.** Focused, not diffuse (see §IV-B on differential from PPD), but operative: the persecutory frame around Captain America organizes perception. Cap is not encountered as a soldier who once destroyed a lab; Cap is *the persecutor* whose existence is the ongoing injury.
- **Sadism.** The choice of Adhesive X as the signature weapon — a substance that immobilizes and entombs without killing immediately — is sadistically signed. Subjects are not destroyed; they are *fixed in place*, conscious, unable to act, mirroring (one can infer) the bonded hood's own phenomenology. The compound is autobiographical.

Kernberg's additional dimension — the integration of aggression into a coherent grandiose self — is the diagnostic key. This is what distinguishes him from simpler antisocial profiles. The aggression *serves* the self; it does not fragment it.

### C. Structural-Dynamic Formulation (Object-Relations)

Underneath the DSM checklist, the structural picture is a *pathological grandiose self* in Kernberg's sense: a fused, defensive amalgam of the ideal self, the ideal object, and the actual self, sealed off against the more vulnerable depressive and persecutory affects that would otherwise surface. This formation is *stable* — which is why he is not a borderline-level personality, despite the affective volatility under stress — but **brittle at its single load-bearing point**, which is the inviolability of the body and face.

When the lab fell and the cowl bonded, the wound landed precisely on the load-bearing point. The grandiose self could not integrate the injury (that would require admitting an inferior had ruined him) and could not collapse into mourning (the structure does not permit it). The only available metabolic pathway was **externalization**: re-locate the injury into the enemy and pursue it there. Hence the obsession.

---

## III. COMORBID: ANTISOCIAL PERSONALITY DISORDER FEATURES

The subject meets criteria for ASPD on the surface — disregard for the rights of others, deceitfulness, recklessness, lack of remorse, failure to conform to social norms — but ASPD as primary undersells him for two reasons:

1. **The crimes are organized around meaning, not opportunity.** ASPD criminality is typically diffuse, opportunistic, and short-horizon. Heinrich's is monothematic, long-horizon (decades), and structured around an ideological self-concept.

2. **The childhood conduct-disorder requirement is met but is itself a function of the dynastic culture.** Per collateral on the Zemo family pattern (V-Battalion historical files), cruelty toward serfs was an enculturated norm in the Zemo household. The child Heinrich's conduct disturbances would be indistinguishable from acculturation. This complicates but does not vitiate the ASPD analog; it shifts the etiology from individual psychopathology toward developmental indoctrination.

ASPD features are therefore noted as **comorbid, behavioral-expression-level**, with NPD-malignant as the structural primary.

---

## IV. AXIS I ANALOG: PERSISTENT GRIEVANCE-REVENGE SYNDROME

This is the *active clinical syndrome* — the thing that, if Heinrich walked into a clinic, would be presenting. The personality disorder is the soil; this is what is growing.

### A. Phenomenology

- **Single identifiable target.** Captain America. Targeting is exclusive; there is no record of a secondary obsession.
- **Single precipitating event.** The lab destruction and Adhesive X bonding. The precipitant is real, reality-anchored, and proportionate to the disturbance only if one accepts the subject's pre-existing narcissistic premises.
- **Monothematic ideation.** All thought returns to the target. Recruitment, science, geography, daily routine — all subordinated.
- **Escalation, not extinction.** Failed attempts do not extinguish the behavior; they accelerate it. This is the diagnostic signature of fixated obsession as distinct from rational adversariality.
- **Loss of secondary goals.** He does not pursue Reich-restoration, personal wealth beyond what funds the obsession, political power, or even the validation of his scientific work outside the revenge frame. Secondary goals have collapsed into the primary.
- **Willingness to die in pursuit.** Demonstrated. The hillside death is the syndromic endpoint.

### B. Mullen Typology Mapping

Per Mullen, Pathé & Purcell's stalker typology, Heinrich maps cleanly to the **resentful/grievance-driven** subtype, with the modifications that (i) the target is a public figure rather than an intimate, and (ii) the grievance is anchored in a genuine, severe, irreversible physical injury rather than a perceived slight. This places him in the most dangerous and least extinguishable category, with the additional feature — uncharacteristic of most grievance stalkers — of substantial technical and organizational resources.

### C. Course

- **Onset:** Acute, identifiable, dated to the Adhesive X incident.
- **Duration:** Lifelong; never in remission.
- **Trajectory:** Progressive worsening; widening of acceptable collateral damage; narrowing of the self around the obsession.
- **Termination:** Death in pursuit. The syndrome did not end before the subject did.

---

## V. AXIS I ANALOG: ATYPICAL POST-TRAUMATIC REORGANIZATION

PTSD as written (DSM-5-TR 309.81) requires re-experiencing, avoidance, negative cognition/mood alterations, and arousal/reactivity, persistent more than one month. The subject formally meets only the *Criterion A* event criterion (exposure to actual serious injury) and partial criteria on hyperarousal (irritability, hypervigilance regarding Cap-related stimuli).

He does **not** show:
- Avoidance of trauma reminders — he *seeks* them, wears one as skin.
- The numbing/anhedonia cluster — his goal-pursuit energy is undiminished.
- Classical flashbacks or dissociative re-experiencing.

What he shows instead is **trauma metabolized into mission** — a presentation seen in subgroups of narcissistically organized trauma survivors where the injury cannot be admitted as injury. The reorganization is total; the wound is recoded as identity (the hood as emblem rather than scar) and the perpetrator as nemesis (Cap as defining other). This is, in the clinical literature on perpetrator-as-other identity reformation, the most refractory possible response to an irreversible trauma. It cannot be treated by extinction (no exposure works on a stimulus that *is* one's body) and cannot be treated by reframing (the narcissistic substrate forbids it).

---

## VI. SOMATIC CONTRIBUTIONS (AXIS III WITH PSYCHIATRIC SEQUELAE)

The bonded cowl is not merely an aesthetic fact; it is a continuous psychophysiological input:

- **Chronic pain at the cloth-tissue interface.** Predicted to produce baseline irritability, lowered frustration tolerance, sleep fragmentation, and a chronic substrate of dysphoria that the subject would not name as such.
- **Sensory occlusion (partial auditory, partial visual peripheral, severe olfactory).** Predicts hypervigilance compensations, paranoid-feeling perceptual gaps, and probable startle exaggeration.
- **Thermal dysregulation.** Predicts heat-related affective lability in the equatorial environment chosen for his base — an environmental choice that, given the dysregulation, looks like self-punishment as much as concealment.
- **Loss of facial reciprocity.** No mirror experience, no being-seen experience, no being-touched-on-face experience. The dermatological literature on facial disfigurement establishes severe risk of depressive and avoidant sequelae; Heinrich's narcissistic structure converts these into rage and pursuit rather than withdrawal, but the *substrate* of facial-recognition-deprivation is the same.

The body, in other words, is feeding the psychiatric picture continuously. Any treatment plan that did not address the somatic input would fail; no such treatment plan was ever offered to him, and his structure would have refused it.

---

## VII. ETIOLOGICAL FORMULATION (FOUR-FACTOR)

A standard biopsychosocial-developmental etiology breakdown:

- **Predisposing (developmental):** Dynastic grooming into entitlement, cruelty, and biological-superiority ideology. Probable temperamental contribution (high baseline trait dominance; low trait agreeableness — both partially heritable, both demonstrated again in the son). Absence of warm attachment figures in early life.
- **Precipitating:** The destruction of the laboratory and the Adhesive X bonding. A single, dated, irreversible event. Without this event, the subject would likely have been a high-functioning malignantly-narcissistic war criminal — destructive, certainly, but not monothematically fixated.
- **Perpetuating:** The cowl itself — continuous tactile reminder; the loss of comrades and rank with the war's end (no group to dilute or check the obsession); the choice of jungle isolation (no social-feedback correction); the success of the early Masters of Evil convocations in producing *almost* a satisfying confrontation (intermittent reinforcement).
- **Protective:** Effectively none. Intellectual capacity could have been protective if turned to other ends; instead it was instrumentalized into the obsession. His son could have been protective; instead the son was indoctrinated and incorporated into the obsession's transmission.

---

## VIII. COURSE OVER TIME

- **Pre-war (1930s):** Aristocratic scientist phase. Personality disorder structurally present, behaviorally subclinical in terms of explicit revenge syndrome. Cruelty expressed through institutional channels (the Reich's racial-scientific apparatus) without personal monothematicism.
- **War period (1939–1945):** Operational period. The hood is adopted after partisan disfigurement. The personality structure consolidates around the wartime uniform-and-rank scaffolding; aggression is socially sanctioned and externally regulated. Lethality high but organized.
- **Disfigurement event:** The lab destruction. The grievance syndrome onsets.
- **Jungle period (post-war through *Avengers* #4):** The obsession crystallizes in isolation. No social check; no opportunity for the wound to be re-narrated by anyone outside himself. The Amazonian compound functions as an echo chamber. This is the period in which the syndrome moves from acute injury to chronic monothematic structure.
- **Resurfacing period (*Avengers* #4–#15):** The behaviors become observable to the historical record. Escalation ladder runs in real time. Approximately one calendar year, possibly less, from re-emergence to death. The compressed timeline is itself diagnostic — the syndrome, denied its target for two decades, runs through its escalation with extraordinary speed once contact is re-established.
- **Death:** Hillside, mid-pursuit, by his own discharged weapon causing a rockslide. The death is *configurationally* the syndrome's terminus: motion toward target, weapon in hand, no satisfaction achieved, no witnesses, no dignity. The narcissistic structure receives, in its final seconds, the exact injury it spent twenty years organizing against — humiliation without audience.

---

## IX. DIFFERENTIAL DIAGNOSIS — WHAT HE IS NOT, AND WHY

### A. Not Antisocial Personality Disorder as primary

- ASPD presupposes a diffuse, opportunistic, short-horizon criminal organization of behavior. Heinrich's organization is monothematic, long-horizon, ideologically structured. The crimes have meaning to him in a way ASPD crimes typically do not have meaning to ASPD subjects.
- ASPD subjects typically lack the stable grandiose self-structure Heinrich displays. Identity in ASPD is shallow and chameleonic; Heinrich's is rigid and continuous across decades.
- ASPD features are nonetheless present and noted as comorbid.

### B. Not Paranoid Personality Disorder

- PPD requires pervasive distrust and suspiciousness of others, generalized across relationships and situations. Heinrich's persecutory cognition is *focused* — one target, one grievance, one origin event. He works with allies, recruits subordinates, manages a household; none of these are characterized by the diffuse suspiciousness PPD requires.
- The persecutory belief is also *reality-anchored* — Cap did destroy his lab; the cowl is bonded. The pathology lies in the meaning assigned and the response organized, not in fabricated suspicion.

### C. Not Psychopathy (Hare PCL-R high-scoring profile)

This is the most important differential and the most counterintuitive. Superficially he reads as a high-PCL-R profile: cold affect, lack of remorse, manipulation, grandiosity, parasitic lifestyle (in the jungle), criminal versatility. But the diagnostic key for primary psychopathy is **affective shallowness combined with rational self-interest under stress** — the prediction that, faced with a sufficiently costly pursuit, the true psychopath disengages.

Heinrich does the opposite. He escalates against his own interest, increases personal exposure with each cycle, and dies pursuing on foot. This is not the behavior of a primary psychopath; it is the behavior of a malignantly narcissistic obsessive whose affective life is *not* shallow but *encysted* — sealed off behind narcissistic defenses, but enormously powerful when activated. The Cap stimulus activates it every time. A psychopath would have walked away in 1948 and rebuilt in Argentina under a new name with a new face beneath a new hood.

The PCL-R Factor 2 items (impulsivity, irresponsibility, behavioral dyscontrol) are also poorly fit; he is *over-controlled* in domains that don't touch the obsession, and dyscontrolled only along the obsession's vector.

### D. Not a Delusional Disorder

- Reality-testing is intact. The cowl is real. The destruction of the lab happened. Captain America exists and is opposing him. There is no false fixed belief in the Karl Jaspers sense.
- The pathology is in the *meaning structure* and the *behavioral response*, both of which can be substantial pathology without delusion.

### E. Not a Primary Mood Disorder

- No anhedonia. Goal-pursuit energy is sustained and high.
- No psychomotor retardation; no diurnal variation pattern; no neurovegetative cluster.
- The grief is encysted, not pervasive, and is expressed as rage-pursuit rather than depressive syndrome.
- A depressive substrate is *possible* (the somatic load alone would predispose), but if present, it is heavily defended and not the active picture.

### F. Not an Anxiety Disorder

- Hypervigilance is present but is narrowly task-specific (operational caution) rather than free-floating.
- No panic phenomena reported. No avoidance pattern.
- The defensive structure is rage-organized rather than fear-organized.

### G. Not OCD

- The obsession is *ego-syntonic*. He does not experience the Cap-fixation as intrusive, unwanted, or distressing-in-itself; he experiences it as his life's purpose. OCD requires ego-dystonic obsession and compulsions performed for relief. The narcissistic obsession does not have this structure.
- Behaviorally there is no record of cleaning, checking, counting, symmetry, or other classical OCD compulsions. The trophy-keeping of Bucky's mask is sentimental-narcissistic, not compulsive.

### H. Not Schizotypal or Schizoid Personality Disorder

- He is sociable when sociability serves him; he commands, recruits, courts. The interpersonal coldness is selective and instrumental, not the diffuse social deficit of schizoid/schizotypal organization.
- No perceptual abnormalities, magical thinking, or odd communicational style. Speech is formal, hyperarticulate, register-elevated.

### I. Not Borderline Personality Organization

- Identity is *over-integrated*, not diffuse. The grandiose self is rigid, not unstable.
- No abandonment-frantic phenomena. Relationships


## Behavioral Atlas

# BEHAVIORAL ATLAS — BARON HEINRICH ZEMO

*Compiled from longitudinal observation across the published record (Sgt. Fury #8; Tales of Suspense #60–68; Avengers #4–15; Captain America #168, #275–278; V-Battalion material; secondary corroboration via Helmut Zemo's filial mimicry). Where direct observation is absent, inference is marked. The catalog is organized by state. Where a tell is conserved across states — i.e. it is structural rather than situational — it is flagged STRUCTURAL.*

---

## I. BASELINE — THE CALM STATE

The calm Zemo is the rarest Zemo on record and the most informative one, because his idle settings are the ones the cowl was meant to hide.

**Posture.** STRUCTURAL. Erect to the point of architectural; shoulders held back and slightly squared, chin elevated approximately ten to fifteen degrees above neutral, weight on the rear foot when stationary. This is the posture of cavalry-school noble training carried into a body that has long since stopped needing it. He does not lean. He does not slump. When standing for extended periods (briefings, interrogations of subordinates, observation of an experiment) he locks the knees rather than shifting weight — an old man's stubbornness against the wear it inflicts.

**Hands.** At rest, clasped behind the small of the back, left wrist held in the right hand — the inspection-walk grip. When seated, fingers steepled or laid flat on the chair-arms; never crossed in the lap (insufficient command-presence), never fidgeting. The hands are kept clean obsessively — the gauntlets come off only for fine laboratory work and are immediately re-donned. INFERENCE: nail-cuticle work is meticulous, performed in private, possibly the only grooming ritual the cowl still permits.

**Gait.** A measured parade-step indoors, slightly heel-heavy, audible on stone or metal flooring. He likes his approach to be heard. Outdoors and in jungle terrain he shortens stride and lowers center-of-mass — the transition is competent and unhurried, indicating substantial fieldcraft beneath the parade affect.

**Voice at rest.** Mid-baritone, slow cadence, full sentences with subordinate clauses intact. The cowl muffles the upper formants; he compensates by enunciating consonants harder than necessary, which produces the clipped, near-theatrical Germanic delivery the record consistently captures. He never trails off. Sentences end on terminal stress, not rising inflection — every declarative is a verdict.

**Eyes.** The only feature visible. They blink less than average (INFERENCE: cowl-edge irritation makes blinking unpleasant; he has trained it down). The gaze tracks slowly and lingers — a noble's appraisal-stare, used on subordinates and enemies indistinguishably. He looks at faces in a fixed pattern: left eye, right eye, mouth, back to left eye — a two-second cycle. Faces of those he considers irrelevant get a single sweep and are then ignored entirely; the person continues to exist as furniture.

**Breathing.** STRUCTURAL. Audibly nasal through the cowl, a constant low whistle-rasp on inhale. He has stopped noticing it. Others have not. This is the single most reliable tell that he is in a room: in any space with reasonable acoustics, his breath precedes him.

**Eating and drinking.** Out of sight, always. INFERENCE: a slit or lifted seam at the lower jaw permits intake; he takes meals alone and at length, and the ritual is humiliating enough that no subordinate has ever been permitted to observe it. The dining room of the jungle compound, by report, has one chair.

**Sleep.** Short and bad. INFERENCE from the cowl's permanence: lying supine compresses the bonded fabric against the scalp; he sleeps semi-reclined, head supported, in a campaign-chair configuration. Likely four to five hours, broken twice. He rises before the workforce.

**Reading.** Voracious and silent. Technical journals, intelligence reports, news clippings about Captain America (saved, dated, annotated in a thin steel-nib hand). He reads with the page held high — not because of eyesight, but because lowering the chin folds the cowl uncomfortably at the throat.

---

## II. WORKING STATE — THE LABORATORY AND THE PLANNING TABLE

This is where Heinrich is most himself, and most stable.

**Affect.** The flattest he gets. Not pleasure — he does not show pleasure — but the absence of strain. The breathing slows. The gaze narrows and focuses. Subordinates who must approach him during work have learned to wait at the threshold; interruption is punished, but interruption *announced and tolerated* (cleared throat, single name) is processed without rancor.

**Manual habits.** He works with the gauntlets off and the cuffs of the tunic folded twice — the only times he ever modifies his dress. Tools are laid out left-to-right in order of use and replaced exactly. Glassware is held by the neck, never the body. He writes equations standing, on vertical surfaces, in chalk or grease pencil; sit-down notation is reserved for prose.

**Verbal tells.** He talks to himself in the lab, in German, in a lower register than his public voice — sentence fragments, chemistry shorthand, the occasional epithet against an absent obstacle. The shift from German private monologue to English public address is automatic and reliable; switching mid-sentence indicates that something has rattled him.

**Decision habit.** In planning, he externalizes. Maps, dossiers, photographs spread across a long table; he walks the length of it, hands behind back, pronouncing alternatives aloud and then striking them down with a single word. He converges on a plan and then does not revisit it — *reconsideration is presented to himself as weakness.* This is the single largest operational vulnerability in his cognitive style: once committed, he will not re-plan, only re-resource.

---

## III. COMMAND STATE — WITH SUBORDINATES

**Greeting protocol.** None for inferiors; an inferior who enters his presence stands and is acknowledged or not, at his pace. Equals — the few he has recognized — receive a shallow nod, never the hand. Physical contact with subordinates is essentially zero across the record.

**Address.** Surnames and titles only. "Herr Garrett." "Madame." "Boy." First names are a privilege he does not grant. Helmut, in childhood, is reportedly addressed by patronymic and family rank as often as by name — corroborated by Helmut's own residual formality of speech.

**Praise.** Almost nonexistent. The highest praise on record is the absence of correction. When praise is issued it is comparative and barbed: "Adequate, for a man of your education." Subordinates competing for it have produced disproportionate work for almost no reinforcement — an exploitative pattern he has refined over decades.

**Correction.** Quiet, surgical, and public. He does not raise his voice to subordinates; he lowers it. The breathing slows, the cadence stretches, and the offender is dissected in front of peers in three to five sentences. He does not strike subordinates personally — the indignity of physical exertion against an inferior is beneath him — but he orders punishment without hesitation and watches it administered.

**Loyalty management.** He does not cultivate loyalty; he assumes it and is surprised when it fails. Defections and captures of the Masters of Evil produce contempt, not introspection. His instinct after a teammate's loss is *replacement at higher tier*, not investigation of the failure. This is the escalation ladder in microcosm.

**Trust calibration.** Trusts no one with the full plan. Each operator receives only the slice required. Even Helmut, in retrospective testimony, was raised on partial information — the ideology delivered whole, the operational history doled out in fragments.

---

## IV. SOCIAL STATE — WITH PEERS AND COURTED ASSETS

The behaviors deployed for Enchantress, Executioner, and other powerful recruits are distinct enough to constitute a separate state.

**Affect.** Courtly. The voice slows further; the consonants soften; the bow appears (a precise fifteen-to-twenty-degree inclination from the waist, hands at sides, eyes never leaving the other party). He kisses no hands — the cowl forbids — but the gesture is mimed in the bow's depth.

**Conversation.** He listens disproportionately in courtship interactions, an unusual departure from baseline. He asks about the interlocutor's grievances and gifts, never about their personal history. He is excellent at making a powerful party feel that their power has finally found a worthy admirer. This is performance and he knows it is performance; the moment the recruit signs on, the courtship vanishes and the command-state replaces it. INFERENCE: he is incapable of sustaining the courtly affect beyond instrumental need, and the transition is abrupt enough to have been noticed by Enchantress, contributing to her eventual disinterest.

**Flattery received.** Visibly metabolized. The chin lifts further; the breathing momentarily quickens; the response is dismissive in word ("Naturally") and acceptant in body. He cannot resist it and is faintly contemptuous of those who deliver it well.

---

## V. INTIMATE STATE — WITH HELMUT, AND THE ABSENCE THEREOF

There is no recorded scene of warmth. The intimate state must be inferred from Helmut's adult presentation and from the few retrospective panels in *Captain America* #168 and #275ff.

**Paternal posture.** Standing over the child, never crouching to his level. Helmut, photographed in childhood, is consistently shown looking up; Heinrich is consistently shown looking forward, past the boy. The boy is addressed, not engaged.

**Pedagogical mode.** Recitation and correction. The child recites the bloodline, the chemistry, the racial doctrine; the father corrects pronunciation and content with equal severity. Errors are not patiently rephrased; they are noted, repeated back, and held against the next recitation. INFERENCE: Helmut's adult perfectionism and intolerance of his own errors are direct inheritances of this regime.

**Physical contact.** A hand on the shoulder is the upper bound on record. No embrace. The cowl makes paternal kiss impossible and provides a permanent alibi for the absence of one Heinrich would not have given regardless.

**Withholding as instrument.** Approval, when it arrives, is brief and contingent. The child learns that performance produces a flicker of acknowledgment and that nothing else does. This produces, in Helmut, the canonical fanatical devotion to a father he barely knew warmly — and this is precisely the instrument Heinrich intended to forge, whether or not he could have articulated it.

---

## VI. STRESS STATE — PLAN UNDER PRESSURE, NOT YET FAILING

When a plan is in motion and beginning to slip:

**Breath.** The nasal rasp shortens. Audible to anyone within three meters.
**Hands.** Move from behind-the-back to in-front clasp, then to the table edge, then to the weapon. The migration is reliable and observable in real time. A subordinate who knows to watch the hands knows exactly how close the room is to violence.
**Speech rate.** Counterintuitively slows further. He compensates for internal acceleration with external deceleration. The cadence becomes ceremonial; the German loanwords increase ("*natürlich*," "*so*," "*Schluss*").
**Eye movement.** The two-second face-cycle breaks. Gaze becomes sticky — locks on a single point (a screen, a map, a face) for ten to twenty seconds. He is computing, and the computation has crowded out tracking.
**Reorganization.** He will redirect resources upward, never re-evaluate aim. New recruits are summoned; new compounds synthesized; new collateral accepted. The plan is the plan.

---
